(function(){
  function hide(){ var el=document.getElementById('boot-loader'); if(!el) return;
    el.classList.add('done'); setTimeout(function(){ el.remove(); },700); }
  if(document.readyState==='complete') setTimeout(hide,200);
  else window.addEventListener('load', function(){ setTimeout(hide,200); });
  setTimeout(hide, 6000); // 兜底：最多 6 秒
})();
</script>

    <div class="rr-frame" id="rr-frame">
      <img src="assets/three-doors.jpg" alt="南山·通道 三门 选择你的身份">
      <!-- 三门呼吸光晕 -->

      <div class="rr-sparks sp-eco"><i></i><i></i><i></i><i></i></div>
      <div class="rr-sparks sp-red"><i></i><i></i><i></i><i></i></div>
      <div class="rr-sparks sp-blue"><i></i><i></i><i></i><i></i></div>
      <!-- 整列热区（门+卡片+按钮） -->
      <div class="rr-hot rr-eco"  role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="青绿之门 红军侦察员 进入探索" onclick="pickDoor('eco')"  onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter')pickDoor('eco')"></div>
      <div class="rr-hot rr-red"  role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="朱红之门 红色草原向导 进入长征" onclick="pickDoor('red')"  onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter')pickDoor('red')"></div>
      <div class="rr-hot rr-blue" role="button" tabindex="0" aria-label="黛蓝之门 机要参谋 进入文化" onclick="pickDoor('blue')" onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter')pickDoor('blue')"></div>
      <!-- 走进门时的彩色闪光 -->
      <div class="rr-flash" id="rr-flash"></div>
    </div>
  </div>
  <script>
  var _doorLock=false;
  function pickDoor(r){
    if(_doorLock) return; _doorLock=true;
    var layer=document.getElementById('roles-ref'), frame=document.getElementById('rr-frame'), flash=document.getElementById('rr-flash');
    var ORIGIN={eco:'26% 45%', red:'50% 42%', blue:'74% 45%'};
    var TINT={eco:'rgba(60,230,110,0.45)', red:'rgba(240,90,50,0.5)', blue:'rgba(80,150,255,0.5)'};
    if(frame){ frame.style.transformOrigin=ORIGIN[r]||'50% 50%'; frame.classList.add('rr-enter'); }
    if(flash){ flash.style.background='radial-gradient(circle at '+(ORIGIN[r]||'50% 50%')+', '+(TINT[r]||'rgba(255,255,255,0.4)')+', transparent 60%)'; flash.classList.add('on'); }
    // 关键：图层先作为不透明"幕布"留在最上层，底下完成旧界面切场后再淡出，
    // 避免旧版三门在切换间隙露出来闪一下
    setTimeout(function(){
      if(typeof selectRole==='function'){ try{ selectRole(r); }catch(e){} }
    }, 680);
    setTimeout(function(){ if(layer) layer.classList.add('rr-leave'); }, 1420);
    setTimeout(function(){ if(layer) layer.style.display='none'; _doorLock=false; }, 1980);
  }
  </script>

// ===== 幕布切换 =====
function showAct(id){
  document.querySelectorAll('.act').forEach(el=>{el.style.display='none';el.style.opacity='0';el.classList.remove('active');});
  const t=document.getElementById(id);
  t.style.display='flex';
  setTimeout(()=>{t.style.opacity='1';t.classList.add('active');},30);
}

// ===== 星星 =====
function genStars(){
  const c=document.getElementById('stars-wrap');
  c.style.cssText='position:fixed;inset:0;pointer-events:none;z-index:0;';
  for(let i=0;i<80;i++){
    const s=document.createElement('div');s.className='star';
    s.style.left=Math.random()*100+'%';
    s.style.top=Math.random()*70+'%';
    c.appendChild(s);
  }
}

// ===== 第一幕入场动画 =====

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  Canvas 云海动画（background-video 效果）
//  layered: 远山 → 云海流动 → 阳光丁达尔 → 近景雾气
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
(function initCloudCanvas(){
  const cvs = document.getElementById('intro-canvas');
  if(!cvs) return;
  const ctx = cvs.getContext('2d');

  function resize(){
    cvs.width  = window.innerWidth;
    cvs.height = window.innerHeight;
  }
  resize();
  window.addEventListener('resize', resize);

  const W = ()=> cvs.width, H = ()=> cvs.height;
  let t = 0;

  // ── 生成柏林噪声简化版（多层正弦叠加）──
  function noise(x, y, seed){
    return (Math.sin(x * 0.012 + seed) * 0.5 +
            Math.sin(x * 0.035 + y * 0.02 + seed * 1.3) * 0.3 +
            Math.sin(x * 0.007 + y * 0.009 + seed * 0.7) * 0.2) * 0.5 + 0.5;
  }

  // ── 云朵粒子 ──
  const clouds = [];
  for(let i = 0; i < 22; i++){
    clouds.push({
      x: Math.random() * 1.6 - 0.3,   // 0~1 相对宽度（超出边缘）
      y: 0.28 + Math.random() * 0.38,  // 云层高度区间
      rx: 0.10 + Math.random() * 0.20, // 横向半径（相对W）
      ry: 0.04 + Math.random() * 0.08, // 纵向半径（相对H）
      speed: 0.000018 + Math.random() * 0.000032,
      alpha: 0.12 + Math.random() * 0.22,
      layer: Math.floor(Math.random() * 3), // 0=远 1=中 2=近
    });
  }

  function drawFrame(){
    t += 0.4;
    const w = W(), h = H();
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);
    // Canvas 仅绘制光效叠加层（mix-blend-mode:screen），不绘制背景色

    // ── 太阳（左上角光晕） ──
    const sunX = w * 0.3, sunY = h * 0.14;
    const sun = ctx.createRadialGradient(sunX, sunY, 0, sunX, sunY, h * 0.45);
    sun.addColorStop(0,    'rgba(255,230,140,0.38)');
    sun.addColorStop(0.18, 'rgba(255,180, 60,0.22)');
    sun.addColorStop(0.42, 'rgba(200,120, 30,0.10)');
    sun.addColorStop(1,    'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
    ctx.fillStyle = sun;
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, w, h);

    // ── 丁达尔光柱 ──
    ctx.save();
    for(let i = 0; i < 7; i++){
      const angle = -0.62 + i * 0.095 + Math.sin(t * 0.003 + i) * 0.012;
      const len   = h * (0.55 + i * 0.04);
      const grd   = ctx.createLinearGradient(
        sunX, sunY,
        sunX + Math.sin(angle) * len,
        sunY + Math.cos(angle) * len
      );
      grd.addColorStop(0,   `rgba(255,220,120,${0.06 + i * 0.005})`);
      grd.addColorStop(0.5, `rgba(255,180, 60,${0.025})`);
      grd.addColorStop(1,   'rgba(255,160,40,0)');
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(sunX, sunY);
      const spread = 0.042 + i * 0.008;
      ctx.lineTo(
        sunX + Math.sin(angle - spread) * len,
        sunY + Math.cos(angle - spread) * len
      );
      ctx.lineTo(
        sunX + Math.sin(angle + spread) * len,
        sunY + Math.cos(angle + spread) * len
      );
      ctx.closePath();
      ctx.fillStyle = grd;
      ctx.fill();
    }
    ctx.restore();

    // ── 云海（多层椭圆，缓慢飘移，叠加在底图上） ──
    clouds.forEach(c => {
      // 位置随时间水平漂移
      const cx = ((c.x + c.speed * t) % 1.6 - 0.3) * w;
      const cy = c.y * h + Math.sin(t * 0.0018 + c.x * 8) * 8;
      const rx = c.rx * w;
      const ry = c.ry * h;

      const grd = ctx.createRadialGradient(cx, cy, 0, cx, cy, rx);
      const base = c.layer === 0 ? 180 : c.layer === 1 ? 200 : 215;
      grd.addColorStop(0,   `rgba(${base},${base+8},${base-5},${c.alpha})`);
      grd.addColorStop(0.5, `rgba(${base-10},${base-5},${base-18},${c.alpha * 0.55})`);
      grd.addColorStop(1,   'rgba(0,0,0,0)');

      ctx.save();
      ctx.scale(1, ry / rx);
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.arc(cx, cy * (rx / ry), rx, 0, Math.PI * 2);
      ctx.fillStyle = grd;
      ctx.fill();
      ctx.restore();
    });

    // 底部雾气省略（底图自带）

    requestAnimationFrame(drawFrame);
  }
  drawFrame();
})();

window.onload=()=>{
  genStars();

  // ── 入场动画时序 ──
  gsap.set(['#intro-title','#intro-sub','#intro-badge','#coin','#ideco'],
    {opacity:0,y:22});

  gsap.timeline({delay:0.6})
    // Canvas 已在跑，0.6s 后开始文字入场
    // 1. 阳光射线渐显
    .to('#sunray',{opacity:0.88,duration:2.2,ease:'power2.out'},0)
    // 2. 主标题从下浮现
    .to('#intro-title',{opacity:1,y:0,duration:1.4,ease:'back.out(1.05)'},0.9)
    // 3. 副标题
    .to('#intro-sub',{opacity:1,y:0,duration:1.0,ease:'power2.out'},1.9)
    // 4. 小徽标行
    .to('#intro-badge',{opacity:1,y:0,duration:0.7,ease:'power2.out'},2.6)
    // 5. 金币弹出
    .to('#coin',{opacity:1,y:0,scale:1,duration:0.9,ease:'back.out(1.8)'},3.1)
    // 6. 底部装饰
    .to('#ideco',{opacity:1,y:0,duration:0.6},3.7);
};

// ===== 语音合成模块 =====
const TTS = {
  synth: window.speechSynthesis,
  voice: null,
  supported: 'speechSynthesis' in window,

  // 初始化：挑选中文语音
  init() {
    if (!this.supported) return;
    const pick = () => {
      const voices = this.synth.getVoices();
      // 优先：zh-CN > zh-TW > zh > 任意
      this.voice =
        voices.find(v => v.lang === 'zh-CN') ||
        voices.find(v => v.lang === 'zh-TW') ||
        voices.find(v => v.lang.startsWith('zh')) ||
        voices[0] || null;
    };
    pick();
    if (this.synth.onvoiceschanged !== undefined) {
      this.synth.onvoiceschanged = pick;
    }
  },

  // 朗读一段文字，完成后调用 onEnd
  speak(text, onEnd) {
    if (!this.supported) { if (onEnd) setTimeout(onEnd, 10); return; }
    this.synth.cancel();
    const utt = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
    if (this.voice) utt.voice = this.voice;
    utt.lang   = 'zh-CN';
    utt.rate   = 0.88;   // 稍慢，沉稳感
    utt.pitch  = 0.95;
    utt.volume = 1;
    utt.onend  = () => { if (onEnd) onEnd(); };
    utt.onerror = () => { if (onEnd) onEnd(); };
    this.synth.speak(utt);
  },

  stop() {
    if (this.supported) this.synth.cancel();
  }
};


// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  视频转场系统
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
let _videoCallback = null;
let _progressTimer = null;

function playTransitionVideo(onEnd){
  _videoCallback = onEnd;
  const wrap  = document.getElementById('transition-video-wrap');
  const video = document.getElementById('transition-video');
  const fadeIn= document.getElementById('tv-fade-in');
  const prog  = document.getElementById('tv-progress');

  if(!wrap || !video) { if(onEnd) onEnd(); return; }

  // 如果不存在第二段占位视频，则动态创建，便于后续替换
  let video2 = document.getElementById('transition-video-2');
  if(!video2){
    video2 = document.createElement('video');
    video2.id = 'transition-video-2';
    video2.preload = 'auto';
    video2.setAttribute('playsinline','');
    video2.setAttribute('webkit-playsinline','');
    video2.style.display = 'none';
    // 占位：无 source，后续可通过设置 `#transition-video-2 src="..."` 替换
    video.parentNode.insertBefore(video2, video.nextSibling);
  }

  // 显示层并准备播放第一段
  wrap.classList.add('active');
  fadeIn.classList.remove('clear');
  prog.style.width = '0%';
  document.getElementById('tv-fade-out').classList.remove('dark');

  // 活动视频引用（用于进度更新）
  let activeVideo = video;
  activeVideo.currentTime = 0;

  // 淡入（黑→视频）
  activeVideo.play().catch(()=>{});
  setTimeout(()=>{ fadeIn.classList.add('clear'); }, 180);

  // 实时更新进度条（基于 activeVideo）
  clearInterval(_progressTimer);
  _progressTimer = setInterval(()=>{
    if(activeVideo && activeVideo.duration){
      prog.style.width = (activeVideo.currentTime / activeVideo.duration * 100) + '%';
    }
  }, 100);

  // 当第一段结束，尝试切换到第二段（仅当已设置 src）
  video.onended = ()=>{
    // 如果第二段可用并有 src，切换播放；否则结束流程
    const hasSrc = (video2 && (video2.currentSrc || video2.querySelector('source')?.src));
    if(hasSrc){
      try{
        // 隐藏第一段，显示第二段
        video.style.display = 'none';
        video2.style.display = '';
        activeVideo = video2;
        activeVideo.currentTime = 0;
        // 绑定结束回调为正式结束
        activeVideo.onended = ()=>{ _finishVideo(); };
        if(activeVideo._timeout) clearTimeout(activeVideo._timeout);
        activeVideo._timeout = setTimeout(()=>{ _finishVideo(); }, 30000);
        activeVideo.play().catch(()=>{});
      }catch(e){ _finishVideo(); }
    } else {
      _finishVideo();
    }
  };

  // 保底：30秒超时（防止video不触发ended）
  if(video._timeout) clearTimeout(video._timeout);
  video._timeout = setTimeout(()=>{ _finishVideo(); }, 30000);
}

function _finishVideo(){
  const v1 = document.getElementById('transition-video');
  const v2 = document.getElementById('transition-video-2');
  const fadeOut= document.getElementById('tv-fade-out');
  const wrap   = document.getElementById('transition-video-wrap');
  clearInterval(_progressTimer);
  if(v1 && v1._timeout){ clearTimeout(v1._timeout); }
  if(v2 && v2._timeout){ clearTimeout(v2._timeout); }

  // 淡出（视频→黑）
  fadeOut.classList.add('dark');
  setTimeout(()=>{
    wrap.classList.remove('active');
    if(v1) try{ v1.pause(); v1.style.display=''; }catch(e){}
    if(v2) try{ v2.pause(); v2.style.display='none'; }catch(e){}
    fadeOut.classList.remove('dark');
    if(_videoCallback){ _videoCallback(); _videoCallback=null; }
  }, 1100);
}

function skipTransitionVideo(){
  const v1 = document.getElementById('transition-video');
  const v2 = document.getElementById('transition-video-2');
  if(v1 && v1._timeout) clearTimeout(v1._timeout);
  if(v2 && v2._timeout) clearTimeout(v2._timeout);
  if(v1) v1.onended = null;
  if(v2) v2.onended = null;
  _finishVideo();
}

TTS.init();

// ===== 启程 =====
function startJourney(){
  const coin=document.getElementById('coin');
  if(coin.style.opacity==='0') return;

  // 金币按下动画
  gsap.to('#coin',{scale:0.88,duration:0.1,yoyo:true,repeat:1,ease:'power2.in',
    onComplete:()=>{
      // 第一幕画面整体压暗
      gsap.to('#act-intro',{filter:'brightness(0)',duration:0.55,ease:'power2.in',
        onComplete:()=>{
          // 播放转场视频，结束后进入叙事
          playTransitionVideo(()=>{
            // 视频结束 → 恢复第一幕亮度（视觉衔接）→ 执行叙事
            document.getElementById('act-intro').style.filter='';
            runNarrative();
          });
        }
      });
    }
  });
}

function runNarrative(){
  // 背景图拉升模糊 → 过渡到地图幕
  gsap.to('#intro-canvas',{scale:1.28,filter:'brightness(1.0) blur(6px)',duration:1.1,ease:'power2.in',
    onComplete:()=>{
      showAct('act-map');
      gsap.fromTo('#map-bg',{filter:'brightness(0)'},{filter:'brightness(1)',duration:2.2,ease:'power2.out'});
      // 隐藏所有UI
      document.querySelectorAll('.poi').forEach(el=>el.style.opacity='0');
      ['left-panel','right-nav','bottom-bar','map-ctrls','scale-bar','score-badge'].forEach(id=>{
        const el=document.getElementById(id);if(el)el.style.opacity='0';
      });

      const nb=document.getElementById('narr-bar');
      const nt=document.getElementById('narr-txt');
      nb.style.opacity='1';
      nb.classList.add('visible');
      let idx=0;

      // 每句：淡出旧文字 → 换内容淡入 + 同步朗读 → 朗读结束后进入下一句
      STATE.narrativeStopped = false;   // 重置中止标志

      (function next(){
        // ── 被跳过时立即中止 ──
        if(STATE.narrativeStopped) return;

        if(idx >= NARR.length){
          TTS.stop();
          gsap.to(nb,{opacity:0,duration:0.8,onComplete:showRoles});
          return;
        }
        const text = NARR[idx++];

        // 文字淡出 → 换内容 → 淡入
        gsap.to(nt,{opacity:0,duration:0.25,onComplete:()=>{
          if(STATE.narrativeStopped) return;   // 淡出过程中被跳过
          nt.textContent = text;
          gsap.to(nt,{opacity:1,duration:0.45,onComplete:()=>{
            if(STATE.narrativeStopped) return; // 淡入过程中被跳过

            let advanced = false;
            // 保底定时器（TTS 不可用时兜底）
            const guard = setTimeout(()=>{
              if(!advanced && !STATE.narrativeStopped){
                advanced = true;
                next();
              }
            }, Math.max(text.length * 220, 2000));

            // 启动波形动画
            document.getElementById('narr-wave').classList.add('active');

            TTS.speak(text, ()=>{
              // 停止波形
              document.getElementById('narr-wave').classList.remove('active');
              if(!advanced && !STATE.narrativeStopped){
                advanced = true;
                clearTimeout(guard);
                setTimeout(next, 380);
              }
            });
          }});
        }});
      })();
    }
  });
}

function skipNarrative(){
  // 1. 立即设置中止标志，阻断 next() 的一切后续调用
  STATE.narrativeStopped = true;
  // 2. 停止语音（同时会触发 utt.onend，但 advanced/narrativeStopped 双重拦截）
  TTS.stop();
  // 3. 停止波形
  document.getElementById('narr-wave').classList.remove('active');
  // 4. 停止叙事文字的所有 gsap 动画
  gsap.killTweensOf('#narr-txt');
  // 5. 淡出叙事条，跳入角色选择
  const nb = document.getElementById('narr-bar');
  nb.classList.remove('visible');
  nb.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
  gsap.to(nb, {opacity:0, duration:0.35, onComplete:showRoles});
}




// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  角色选择 — 史诗奇幻三门演出
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ── 全屏山脉背景（俯瞰山地云海，对标效果图背景） ──
function initRolesBgCanvas(){
  const cvs = document.getElementById('roles-bg-canvas');
  if(!cvs) return;
  function resize(){ cvs.width=window.innerWidth; cvs.height=window.innerHeight; }
  resize(); window.addEventListener('resize',resize);
  const ctx=cvs.getContext('2d'); let t=0;

  function frame(){
    t+=0.3;
    const w=cvs.width, h=cvs.height;
    ctx.clearRect(0,0,w,h);

    // 深夜山地天空
    const sky=ctx.createRadialGradient(w*.5,h*.3,0,w*.5,h*.3,w*.8);
    sky.addColorStop(0,'rgb(16,26,14)'); sky.addColorStop(.45,'rgb(10,18,9)'); sky.addColorStop(1,'rgb(3,5,3)');
    ctx.fillStyle=sky; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);

    // 三色光源（门的颜色，从下方向上漫射，模拟效果图的绿/红/蓝光道）
    [[w*.28,'rgba(30,180,58,'], [w*.50,'rgba(210,50,25,'], [w*.72,'rgba(30,110,240,']].forEach(([cx,c])=>{
      const g=ctx.createRadialGradient(cx,h,0,cx,h,h*.7);
      g.addColorStop(0,c+'0.22)'); g.addColorStop(.45,c+'0.08)'); g.addColorStop(1,c+'0)');
      ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
    });

    // 远山（四层，从远到近，高度递减，颜色递深）
    [[.55,h*.25,.9,'rgba(14,26,12,0.88)',.009],
     [.64,h*.20,.65,'rgba(16,30,14,0.94)',.013],
     [.73,h*.15,.42,'rgba(8,18,7,0.97)',.007],
     [.84,h*.10,.28,'rgba(4,10,4,1.00)',.004]].forEach(([yb,amp,freq,col,spd])=>{
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0,h);
      for(let x=0;x<=w;x+=2){
        const n=Math.sin(x*freq*.003+spd*t)*.5+Math.sin(x*freq*.007+spd*t*.7)*.3+Math.sin(x*freq*.015+spd*t*.5)*.2;
        ctx.lineTo(x, h*yb - (n*.5+.5)*amp);
      }
      ctx.lineTo(w,h); ctx.closePath(); ctx.fillStyle=col; ctx.fill();
    });

    // 云海（中部，16个，缓慢漂移）
    ctx.save(); ctx.globalAlpha=0.55;
    for(let i=0;i<16;i++){
      const cx=((i*138.5+t*.2)%w);
      const cy=h*(.38+Math.sin(i*.65)*.1);
      const rx=90+i*18, ry=22+i*4;
      const g=ctx.createRadialGradient(cx,cy,0,cx,cy,rx);
      g.addColorStop(0,'rgba(175,195,165,0.14)'); g.addColorStop(.5,'rgba(150,170,140,0.07)'); g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.save(); ctx.scale(1,ry/rx);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy*(rx/ry),rx,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fill();
      ctx.restore();
    }
    ctx.restore();

    // 星点（顶部 1/3 区域）
    ctx.save();
    for(let i=0;i<32;i++){
      const sx=(Math.sin(i*73.1)*.5+.5)*w, sy=(Math.cos(i*47.3)*.5+.5)*h*.42;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(sx,sy,.8,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(195,215,188,${.22+Math.sin(t*.04+i*1.3)*.14})`; ctx.fill();
    }
    ctx.restore();

    requestAnimationFrame(frame);
  }
  frame();
}

// ── 门内世界 Canvas ──
function initPortalCanvas(id, type){
  const cvs=document.getElementById(id); if(!cvs) return;
  const p=cvs.parentElement, r=p.getBoundingClientRect();
  cvs.width=Math.max(r.width||150,150); cvs.height=Math.max(r.height||280,280);
  const ctx=cvs.getContext('2d'); let t=0;

  const worlds={
    // 草原湿地：晨光绿野、溪流、飞鸟
    eco(ctx,w,h,t){
      // 天空
      const sky=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,h*.55);
      sky.addColorStop(0,'#0d2a10'); sky.addColorStop(.55,'#1e5222'); sky.addColorStop(1,'#2a6830');
      ctx.fillStyle=sky; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
      // 晨光
      const sg=ctx.createRadialGradient(w*.42,h*.06,0,w*.42,h*.06,h*.62);
      sg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(188,255,148,0.28)'); sg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.fillStyle=sg; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
      // 远山
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0,h);
      for(let x=0;x<=w;x+=2) ctx.lineTo(x, h*.52-Math.sin(x*.022+.4)*h*.1-Math.sin(x*.008)*h*.05);
      ctx.lineTo(w,h); ctx.lineTo(0,h); ctx.closePath();
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(14,44,17,0.9)'; ctx.fill();
      // 草地
      const grd=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,h*.5,0,h);
      grd.addColorStop(0,'#1e5822'); grd.addColorStop(1,'#0c2a10');
      ctx.fillStyle=grd; ctx.fillRect(0,h*.5,w,h*.5);
      // 草浪
      for(let i=0;i<7;i++){
        const y=h*(.52+i*.072);
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0,y);
        for(let x=0;x<=w;x+=2) ctx.lineTo(x,y+Math.sin(x*.065+t*.022+i*.88)*4.5);
        ctx.strokeStyle=`rgba(42,${148+i*10},50,${.58-i*.06})`; ctx.lineWidth=1.8; ctx.stroke();
      }
      // 溪流（蜿蜒）
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(w*.35,h*.52);
      ctx.bezierCurveTo(w*.4,h*.6, w*.45,h*.68, w*.38,h*.78);
      ctx.bezierCurveTo(w*.32,h*.88, w*.42,h*.92, w*.5,h);
      ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(48,200,160,0.38)'; ctx.lineWidth=4; ctx.stroke();
      // 湿地水面
      const wg=ctx.createRadialGradient(w*.5,h*.74,0,w*.5,h*.74,w*.38);
      wg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(20,85,58,0.55)'); wg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.fillStyle=wg; ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(w*.5,h*.74,w*.36,h*.055,0,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
      // 水面光纹
      for(let i=0;i<4;i++){
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(w*(.3+i*.12),h*.74+Math.sin(t*.04+i)*1.5, 8+i*4, 1.5,0,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(95,230,178,0.22)'; ctx.fill();
      }
      // 飞鸟（5只）
      for(let i=0;i<5;i++){
        const bx=((t*.72+i*58)%(w+24))-12;
        const by=h*.15+i*h*.042+Math.sin(t*.032+i*1.2)*6;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(bx-7,by); ctx.quadraticCurveTo(bx,by-4.5,bx+7,by);
        ctx.strokeStyle=`rgba(155,252,138,${.52+Math.sin(t*.04+i)*.14})`; ctx.lineWidth=1.4; ctx.stroke();
      }
    },

    // 长征：橙红天空、雪山、行军队伍、旗帜
    red(ctx,w,h,t){
      const sky=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,h*.65);
      sky.addColorStop(0,'#1c0504'); sky.addColorStop(.38,'#3e0d09'); sky.addColorStop(1,'#5e1c0e');
      ctx.fillStyle=sky; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
      // 太阳光
      const sg=ctx.createRadialGradient(w*.5,h*.08,0,w*.5,h*.08,h*.58);
      sg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(255,125,48,0.38)'); sg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.fillStyle=sg; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
      // 雪山
      [[w*.5,h*.06,w*.44],[w*.22,h*.18,w*.28],[w*.78,h*.16,w*.25]].forEach(([px,py,pw])=>{
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(px-pw,py+pw*.28); ctx.lineTo(px,py); ctx.lineTo(px+pw,py+pw*.28);
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(248,238,228,0.22)'; ctx.fill();
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(px-pw*.26,py+pw*.12); ctx.lineTo(px,py); ctx.lineTo(px+pw*.26,py+pw*.12);
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,252,248,0.36)'; ctx.fill();
      });
      // 地面
      const grd=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,h*.58,0,h);
      grd.addColorStop(0,'#2e0806'); grd.addColorStop(1,'#120302');
      ctx.fillStyle=grd; ctx.fillRect(0,h*.58,w,h*.42);
      // 地缝裂光
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(222,58,22,0.28)'; ctx.fillRect(0,h*.58,w,h*.04);
      // 行军人群（9人右→左）
      for(let i=0;i<9;i++){
        const bx=w*1.1-((t*.45+i*24)%(w*1.35));
        const by=h*.67+(i%3)*h*.03+Math.sin(t*.1+i)*1.8;
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(18,4,3,0.92)';
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(bx,by,4,8,0,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(bx,by-10,3.8,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(24,6,4,0.88)'; ctx.fill();
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(bx+2,by-4); ctx.lineTo(bx+8,by-14);
        ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(75,28,18,0.62)'; ctx.lineWidth=1.2; ctx.stroke();
      }
      // 旗帜
      const fx=w*.5, fy=h*.28, wv=Math.sin(t*.07)*9;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(fx,fy); ctx.lineTo(fx,fy+h*.3);
      ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(155,118,78,0.72)'; ctx.lineWidth=1.8; ctx.stroke();
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(fx,fy);
      ctx.bezierCurveTo(fx+w*.2+wv,fy+4, fx+w*.18+wv,fy+20, fx,fy+25);
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(218,24,14,0.94)'; ctx.fill();
      // 五角星
      const [sx,sy,sr]=[fx+11,fy+9,5.5];
      ctx.beginPath();
      for(let i=0;i<5;i++){
        const a=i*Math.PI*2/5-Math.PI/2, b=a+Math.PI/5;
        i===0?ctx.moveTo(sx+Math.cos(a)*sr,sy+Math.sin(a)*sr):ctx.lineTo(sx+Math.cos(a)*sr,sy+Math.sin(a)*sr);
        ctx.lineTo(sx+Math.cos(b)*sr*.4,sy+Math.sin(b)*sr*.4);
      }
      ctx.closePath(); ctx.fillStyle='rgba(252,222,30,0.96)'; ctx.fill();
    },

    // 侗族夜景：蓝紫夜空、多层鼓楼、风雨桥、月光水面
    blue(ctx,w,h,t){
      const sky=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,h*.72);
      sky.addColorStop(0,'#020412'); sky.addColorStop(.5,'#040820'); sky.addColorStop(1,'#060c2c');
      ctx.fillStyle=sky; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
      // 月亮
      const mx=w*.72, my=h*.1;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(mx,my,13,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fillStyle='rgba(210,236,255,0.8)'; ctx.fill();
      const mg=ctx.createRadialGradient(mx,my,0,mx,my,h*.4);
      mg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(155,210,255,0.24)'); mg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.fillStyle=mg; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
      // 星点
      for(let i=0;i<28;i++){
        const sx=(Math.sin(i*97.3)*.5+.5)*w, sy=(Math.cos(i*137.5)*.5+.5)*h*.55;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(sx,sy,.8,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(188,215,255,${.28+Math.sin(t*.05+i*1.1)*.2})`; ctx.fill();
      }
      // 地面
      const grd=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,h*.62,0,h);
      grd.addColorStop(0,'#060c22'); grd.addColorStop(1,'#020408');
      ctx.fillStyle=grd; ctx.fillRect(0,h*.62,w,h*.38);
      // 鼓楼（多层屋顶）
      function tower(tx,ty,tw,layers,stroke){
        for(let i=0;i<layers;i++){
          const rw=tw*(1-i*.16), ry=ty-i*tw*.21;
          ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(tx-rw/2,ry+rw*.17); ctx.lineTo(tx,ry); ctx.lineTo(tx+rw/2,ry+rw*.17);
          ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(3,6,${18+i*4},0.95)`; ctx.fill();
          ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(tx-rw/2,ry+rw*.17); ctx.lineTo(tx+rw/2,ry+rw*.17);
          ctx.strokeStyle=stroke; ctx.lineWidth=1.5; ctx.stroke();
        }
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(2,4,15,0.95)'; ctx.fillRect(tx-tw*.1,ty,tw*.2,tw*.42);
      }
      tower(w*.5, h*.1, w*.62,5,`rgba(48,138,255,${.44+Math.sin(t*.03)*.08})`);
      tower(w*.17,h*.28,w*.36,3,'rgba(38,112,225,0.3)');
      tower(w*.83,h*.3, w*.32,3,'rgba(38,112,225,0.28)');
      // 风雨桥
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(3,6,18,0.9)'; ctx.fillRect(0,h*.7,w,h*.06);
      for(let i=0;i<5;i++){
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(w*(.1+i*.2),h*.7,w*.046,Math.PI,0);
        ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(38,114,225,0.38)'; ctx.lineWidth=1.2; ctx.stroke();
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(w*(.07+i*.2),h*.7); ctx.lineTo(w*(.1+i*.2),h*.67); ctx.lineTo(w*(.13+i*.2),h*.7);
        ctx.fillStyle='rgba(3,6,17,0.92)'; ctx.fill();
      }
      // 水面
      const wg=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,h*.77,0,h*.88);
      wg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(6,16,52,0.62)'); wg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(2,5,18,0.2)');
      ctx.fillStyle=wg; ctx.fillRect(0,h*.77,w,h*.11);
      const mrg=ctx.createRadialGradient(mx,h*.8,0,mx,h*.8,w*.2);
      mrg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(155,212,255,0.22)'); mrg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.fillStyle=mrg; ctx.fillRect(0,h*.77,w,h*.11);
      // 水纹
      for(let i=0;i<5;i++){
        const wy=h*(.79+i*.018)+Math.sin(t*.04+i)*1.8;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(w*.08,wy); ctx.lineTo(w*.92,wy);
        ctx.strokeStyle=`rgba(48,118,205,${.14-i*.02})`; ctx.lineWidth=.9; ctx.stroke();
      }
      // 蓝色粒子
      for(let i=0;i<12;i++){
        const px=((t*.28+i*31)%w), py=h*.38+Math.sin(t*.035+i*.65)*h*.14;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(px,py,1.1,0,Math.PI*2);
        ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(68,172,255,${.28+Math.sin(t*.055+i)*.18})`; ctx.fill();
      }
    }
  };

  function loop(){
    t++;
    const w=cvs.width,h=cvs.height;
    ctx.clearRect(0,0,w,h);
    worlds[type](ctx,w,h,t);
    requestAnimationFrame(loop);
  }
  loop();
}

// ── 10秒预告片时间轴 ──
function showRoles(){
  showAct('act-roles');
  initRolesBgCanvas();
  setTimeout(()=>{
    initPortalCanvas('cvs-eco','eco');
    initPortalCanvas('cvs-red','red');
    initPortalCanvas('cvs-blue','blue');
  },4200);

  const tl=gsap.timeline();

  // 0~2s 标题显现
  tl.to('#roles-title',{opacity:1,y:0,duration:1.1,ease:'power2.out'},0.2);

  // 2~4s 裂缝刺出 + 震动
  tl.to('#ck1',{opacity:1,scaleY:1.5,duration:0.52,ease:'power3.out',transformOrigin:'bottom center'},1.8);
  tl.to('#ck2',{opacity:1,scaleY:1.7,duration:0.58,ease:'power3.out',transformOrigin:'bottom center'},2.0);
  tl.to('#ck3',{opacity:1,scaleY:1.5,duration:0.52,ease:'power3.out',transformOrigin:'bottom center'},2.2);
  tl.call(()=>{
    gsap.to('#act-roles',{x:4,duration:.07,ease:'none',repeat:10,yoyo:true,
      onComplete:()=>gsap.set('#act-roles',{x:0})});
  },null,2.55);

  // 3.9s 裂缝消退
  tl.to(['#ck1','#ck2','#ck3'],{opacity:0,scaleY:2.5,duration:0.32,ease:'power2.in'},3.9);

  // 4~6s 三门破石升起（高潮）
  tl.fromTo(['#pw-eco','#pw-red','#pw-blue'],
    {opacity:0,y:95,scale:0.6,filter:'brightness(3)'},
    {opacity:1,y:0,scale:1,filter:'brightness(1)',duration:1.55,stagger:0.14,ease:'back.out(1.65)'},
    4.05
  );
  // 出现闪光
  tl.fromTo('#act-roles',
    {filter:'brightness(1)'},
    {filter:'brightness(2.6)',duration:.12,yoyo:true,repeat:1,ease:'power2.out'},
    4.1
  );
  // 强震
  tl.call(()=>{
    gsap.to('#act-roles',{x:8,duration:.055,ease:'none',repeat:9,yoyo:true,
      onComplete:()=>gsap.set('#act-roles',{x:0,y:0})});
  },null,4.15);

  // 6~8s 地面能量光道
  tl.to(['#road-eco','#road-red','#road-blue'],
    {opacity:1,duration:1.2,stagger:0.14,ease:'power2.out'},6.0);
  // 门框脉冲
  tl.to('.portal-aura',
    {opacity:.9,duration:.6,ease:'sine.inOut',yoyo:true,repeat:1,stagger:.12},6.3);

  // 边缘高亮显现并扫光（rim sweep）
  tl.to('.portal-rim', {opacity:1, scale:1, duration:0.6, stagger:0.12, ease:'power2.out'}, 6.45);
  tl.to('.portal-rim .rim-sweep', {opacity:1, duration:1.85, stagger:0.12, ease:'sine.inOut'}, 6.6);
  // 门名轻微脉冲以增强视觉焦点
  tl.to('.portal-name', {scale:1.04, duration:0.45, yoyo:true, repeat:1, ease:'power1.inOut'}, 6.8);
  // aura 旋转与微幅抖动加强能量感
  tl.to('.portal-aura', {rotation:6, duration:1.2, yoyo:true, repeat:1, stagger:0.12, ease:'sine.inOut'}, 6.55);

  // 8~10s 角色卡浮现
  tl.fromTo(['#pc-eco','#pc-red','#pc-blue'],
    {opacity:0,y:24},
    {opacity:1,y:0,duration:.75,stagger:.16,ease:'back.out(1.5)'},8.0);
  tl.to('#roles-hint',{opacity:1,duration:.8,ease:'power2.out'},9.0);

  // 解锁点击
  tl.call(()=>{
    document.getElementById('portals-stage').style.pointerEvents='auto';
    document.querySelectorAll('.portal-wrap').forEach(el=>el.style.pointerEvents='auto');
  },null,8.6);
}

// ===== 进入地图模式（POI + UI 全部显示） =====
function enterMapMode(){
  try{revealDashboard();}catch(_){}
  // 隐藏叙事条
  const nb = document.getElementById('narr-bar');
  if(nb) nb.style.opacity = '0';

  // 左侧面板滑入
  gsap.fromTo('#left-panel',
    {x:-255, opacity:0},
    {x:0, opacity:1, duration:0.9, ease:'power3.out'}
  );
  // 积分徽章
  gsap.to('#score-badge', {opacity:1, duration:0.5, delay:0.4});
  // 右侧导航
  gsap.fromTo('#right-nav',
    {x:75, opacity:0},
    {x:0, opacity:1, duration:0.7, delay:0.5, ease:'back.out(1.2)'}
  );
  // 底部控制台
  gsap.fromTo('#bottom-bar',
    {y:65, opacity:0},
    {y:0, opacity:1, duration:0.8, delay:0.3, ease:'back.out(1.2)'}
  );
  // 地图控件
  gsap.fromTo('#map-ctrls',
    {x:55, opacity:0},
    {x:0, opacity:1, duration:0.6, delay:0.6}
  );
  // 比例尺
  gsap.to('#scale-bar', {opacity:1, duration:0.5, delay:0.7});

  // POI 点位逐个弹出（关键：从 opacity:0 → 1）
  document.querySelectorAll('.poi').forEach((el, i) => {
    el.style.opacity = '0';
    el.style.transform = 'translate(-50%,-50%) scale(0.3)';
    setTimeout(() => {
      gsap.fromTo(el,
        {scale:0.3, opacity:0},
        {scale:1, opacity:1, duration:0.55, ease:'back.out(1.7)',
         onStart: () => { el.style.transform = ''; }}
      );
    }, 850 + i * 200);
  });
}

function selectRole(role){
  STATE.role=role;
  const nm={eco:'红军侦察员·山地环境观察员',red:'红色草原向导·社区共管宣导员',blue:'机要参谋·全域资源研究员'};
  const pw=document.getElementById('pw-'+role);
  if(pw) gsap.to(pw,{scale:1.06,filter:'brightness(1.75)',duration:.25,yoyo:true,repeat:1});
  setTimeout(()=>{
    showAct('act-map');
    gsap.fromTo('#map-bg',{filter:'brightness(0)'},{filter:'brightness(1)',duration:1.8,ease:'power2.out'});
    setTimeout(enterMapMode,900);
    setTimeout(()=>setActiveDoor(role),950);
    showToast('🎖️','身份确认',nm[role]+' —— 任务开始！');
  },360);
}

// ===== 主题切换 =====
function selectTheme(t){
  STATE.role=t;                       // 门 = 身份：绿=侦察员 红=向导 蓝=机要参谋
  setActiveDoor(t);
  gsap.fromTo('#map-bg',{filter:'brightness(1.15)'},{filter:'brightness(1)',duration:0.8});
  showToast(ROLE_ICONS[t]||'🎖️','身份切换：'+ROLE_LABELS[t], ROLE_DOORS[t]+' · 点击点位查看'+ROLE_LABELS[t]+'专属任务');
  if(typeof TEAM_MEMBERS_DATA!=='undefined'&&TEAM_MEMBERS_DATA[0]) TEAM_MEMBERS_DATA[0].role=t;
  const ov=document.getElementById('poi-ov');
  if(curPOI&&ov&&ov.classList.contains('show')) openPOI(curPOI);   // 实时刷新已打开的点位任务
  if(typeof _openRPanel!=='undefined'&&_openRPanel==='task'){ try{updateTaskRing();renderTaskList(_taskTab);}catch(_){} }
}

function poiTaskRows(k,arr){
  return arr.map(tk=>`<div class="trow" onclick="doTask('${k}','${tk.n}',${tk.p})"><div class="ti">${tk.i}</div><div class="tt"><strong>${tk.n}</strong><span>${tk.d}</span></div><div class="tp">+${tk.p}</div></div>`).join('');
}
function buildPOIBody(k,d){
  const role=STATE.role||'eco';
  const rt=POI_ROLE_TASKS[k];
  let html='<p>'+d.intro+'</p>';
  html+=`<div class="poi-role-badge">${ROLE_ICONS[role]} 当前身份：<b>${ROLE_LABELS[role]}</b>　·　${ROLE_DOORS[role]}</div>`;
  if(rt){
    const mine=rt[role];
    if(mine&&mine.length){
      html+=`<div class="poi-sec-h role">▎ ${ROLE_LABELS[role]}专属任务</div><div class="task-list">${poiTaskRows(k,mine)}</div>`;
    }
    if(rt.shared&&rt.shared.length){
      html+=`<div class="poi-sec-h shared">▎ 全员共同任务</div><div class="task-list">${poiTaskRows(k,rt.shared)}</div>`;
    }
    if((!mine||!mine.length)&&(!rt.shared||!rt.shared.length)){
      html+=`<div class="poi-sec-h role">▎ 可用任务</div><div class="task-list">${poiTaskRows(k,d.tasks||[])}</div>`;
    }
  } else {
    html+=`<div class="poi-sec-h role">▎ 可用任务</div><div class="task-list">${poiTaskRows(k,d.tasks||[])}</div>`;
  }
  return html;
}
function setActiveDoor(role){
  document.querySelectorAll('.mtb-center .door').forEach(x=>x.classList.remove('door-active'));
  const cls={eco:'door-eco',red:'door-red',blue:'door-blue'}[role];
  if(cls){ const el=document.querySelector('.mtb-center .'+cls); if(el) el.classList.add('door-active'); }
}

function openPOI(k){
  const d=POIS[k];if(!d)return;curPOI=k;
  document.getElementById('mhico').textContent=d.ico;
  document.getElementById('mhico').style.background=d.c;
  document.getElementById('mtitle').textContent=d.t;
  document.getElementById('msub').textContent=d.s;
  const body=document.getElementById('mbody');
  body.innerHTML=buildPOIBody(k,d);
  document.getElementById('poi-ov').classList.add('show');
  gsap.fromTo('#map-bg',{scale:STATE.mapScale},{scale:STATE.mapScale*1.04,duration:0.5,ease:'power2.out',yoyo:true,repeat:1});
  try{updateInfoCard(k);}catch(_){}
}
function closePOI(e){if(!e||e.target===document.getElementById('poi-ov'))document.getElementById('poi-ov').classList.remove('show');}
function enterPOI(){
  closePOI();
  if(curPOI&&!STATE.completedPOIs.includes(curPOI))STATE.completedPOIs.push(curPOI);
  if(curPOI==='huangdu'&&typeof enterBlueWorld==='function'){ enterBlueWorld(); return; }
  showToast('🏛️','已进入展馆',POIS[curPOI]?.t+' 探索开始');
  if(Math.random()>0.4)setTimeout(triggerSp,1400);
}
function doTask(k,nm,pts){
  addScore(pts);showToast('✅','任务完成',nm+' +'+pts+'分');
  closePOI();
  if(Math.random()>0.5&&pts>=30)setTimeout(triggerSp,900);
}

// ===== 物种图鉴 =====
function triggerSp(){
  const sp=SPECIES[Math.floor(Math.random()*SPECIES.length)];
  document.getElementById('sp-head').style.background=`linear-gradient(135deg,${sp.gc}22,${sp.gc}44)`;
  document.getElementById('sp-gr').textContent=sp.gr;
  document.getElementById('sp-gr').style.color=sp.gc;
  document.getElementById('sp-gr').style.borderColor=sp.gc;
  document.getElementById('sp-ico').textContent=sp.ic;
  document.getElementById('sp-nm').textContent=sp.n;
  document.getElementById('sp-sc').textContent=sp.sc;
  document.getElementById('sp-ds').textContent=sp.d;
  document.getElementById('sp-pt').innerHTML=`🌿 新增 <strong>+${sp.p}</strong> NSP · 已录入生态图鉴`;
  document.getElementById('sp-ov').classList.add('show');
  addScore(sp.p);
}
function closeSp(){document.getElementById('sp-ov').classList.remove('show');}

// ===== 积分 =====
function addScore(pts){
  STATE.score+=pts;
  const el=document.getElementById('sval');
  const end=STATE.score;let cur=parseInt(el.textContent)||0;
  const step=Math.ceil((end-cur)/20);
  const iv=setInterval(()=>{cur=Math.min(cur+step,end);el.textContent=cur;if(cur>=end)clearInterval(iv);},30);
}

// ===== 昼夜 =====
function toggleNight(){
  STATE.isNight=!STATE.isNight;
  document.body.classList.toggle('night-mode',STATE.isNight);
  document.querySelectorAll('.star').forEach(s=>s.style.opacity=STATE.isNight?(Math.random()*0.5+0.2).toFixed(2):'0');
  document.getElementById('night-lbl').textContent=STATE.isNight?'白昼模式':'昼夜模式';
  const ico=document.querySelector('#night-ctrl i');
  ico.className=STATE.isNight?'fa-solid fa-moon':'fa-solid fa-sun';
  ico.style.color=STATE.isNight?'#a0b4e0':'#f0d080';
  showToast(STATE.isNight?'🌙':'☀️',STATE.isNight?'夜幕降临':'旭日东升',STATE.isNight?'进入夜间模式':'切换白昼模式');
}

// ===== 缩放/视角 =====
function applyT(){gsap.to('#map-bg',{scale:STATE.mapScale,x:STATE.mx,y:STATE.my,duration:0.4,ease:'power2.out'});}
function zoomIn(){STATE.mapScale=Math.min(STATE.mapScale+0.15,2.4);applyT();}
function zoomOut(){STATE.mapScale=Math.max(STATE.mapScale-0.15,0.7);applyT();}
function toggle3D(){
  STATE.is3D=!STATE.is3D;
  document.getElementById('v2d').textContent=STATE.is3D?'3D':'2D';
  gsap.to('#map-bg',{rotateX:STATE.is3D?10:0,perspective:STATE.is3D?1000:0,duration:0.6,ease:'power2.inOut'});
  showToast('🗺️','视角切换',STATE.is3D?'3D鸟瞰视角':'2D平面视角');
}

// ════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  功能面板系统：天气 / 昼夜 / 组队 / GPS

// ── 面板开关 ──────────────────────────────────────
const PANELS = ['weather','daynight','team','gps'];
let _openPanel = null;

function togglePanel(name){
  if(_openPanel === name){ closePanel(name); return; }
  if(_openPanel) closePanel(_openPanel, false);
  _openPanel = name;
  const el = document.getElementById('panel-'+name);
  if(!el) return;
  el.classList.add('open');
  // 打开时初始化内容
  if(name==='weather')  initWeatherPanel();
  if(name==='daynight') initDayNightPanel();
  if(name==='team')     initTeamPanel();
  if(name==='gps')      initGPSPanel();
  // 点外部关闭
  setTimeout(()=>{
    const handler = e=>{
      if(!el.contains(e.target) && !e.target.closest('.ctrl')){
        closePanel(name); document.removeEventListener('click',handler);
      }
    };
    document.addEventListener('click', handler);
  }, 150);
}

function closePanel(name, resetOpen=true){
  const el = document.getElementById('panel-'+name);
  if(el) el.classList.remove('open');
  if(resetOpen) _openPanel = null;
}

// ── 天气面板 ──────────────────────────────────────
const WEATHER_DATA = {
  // 南山通道真实气候参考数据（随机微浮动）
  base:{ temp:18, humid:72, wind:'NE 3级', vis:'15km', press:'1013hPa', feel:16, uv:'UV 3（中）' },
  forecast:[
    {day:'今天', icon:'⛅', high:20, low:13},
    {day:'明天', icon:'🌦', high:17, low:11},
    {day:'后天', icon:'☀️', high:22, low:14},
    {day:'周四',  icon:'⛅', high:19, low:12},
    {day:'周五',  icon:'🌧', high:15, low:10},
  ],
  icons:{ sunny:'☀️', cloudy:'⛅', rainy:'🌧', foggy:'🌫', snowy:'❄️', thunder:'⛈' }
};

let _weatherTimer = null;
function initWeatherPanel(){
  const d = WEATHER_DATA.base;
  const float = (v,r)=> (v + (Math.random()-0.5)*r*2).toFixed(1);
  const t = Math.round(float(d.temp, 1.5));

  document.getElementById('w-temp').textContent   = t;
  document.getElementById('w-humid').textContent  = Math.round(float(d.humid, 4))+'%';
  document.getElementById('w-wind').textContent   = d.wind;
  document.getElementById('w-vis').textContent    = d.vis;
  document.getElementById('w-press').textContent  = d.press;
  document.getElementById('w-feel').textContent   = Math.round(t - 2)+'°C';
  document.getElementById('w-uv').textContent     = d.uv;

  // 天气图标（根据时间）
  const h = new Date().getHours();
  let icon = '⛅', cond='多云间晴';
  if(h>=6 && h<10){icon='🌅';cond='晨雾渐散';}
  else if(h>=10&&h<16){icon='☀️';cond='晴朗';}
  else if(h>=16&&h<19){icon='🌇';cond='日落云霞';}
  else {icon='🌙';cond='夜间多云';}
  document.getElementById('w-icon-big').textContent = icon;
  document.getElementById('w-cond').textContent     = cond;
  // 控制台同步
  document.getElementById('w-ctrl-temp').textContent = t+'°C';
  document.getElementById('w-ctrl-cond').textContent  = cond.slice(0,3);

  // 预报条
  const fc = document.getElementById('w-forecast');
  fc.innerHTML = WEATHER_DATA.forecast.map((f,i)=>
    `<div class="wf-day ${i===0?'today':''}">
      <div class="wfd-name">${f.day}</div>
      <div class="wfd-icon">${f.icon}</div>
      <div class="wfd-temp">${f.high}°/${f.low}°</div>
    </div>`
  ).join('');

  // 每30s刷新一次（模拟实时）
  clearInterval(_weatherTimer);
  _weatherTimer = setInterval(()=>{
    if(_openPanel==='weather') initWeatherPanel();
  }, 30000);
}

// ── 昼夜面板 ──────────────────────────────────────
const TIME_PRESETS = {
  dawn:  {hour:6,  label:'🌅 黎明', skyA:'#1a0a30', skyB:'#e06030', bodyY:'20%', body:'🌅', fill:'4%'},
  day:   {hour:12, label:'☀️ 正午', skyA:'#1a5faa', skyB:'#60a8e0', bodyY:'8%',  body:'☀️', fill:'45%'},
  dusk:  {hour:18, label:'🌇 黄昏', skyA:'#300828', skyB:'#c05020', bodyY:'18%', body:'🌇', fill:'80%'},
  night: {hour:22, label:'🌙 深夜', skyA:'#040412', skyB:'#0a0820', bodyY:'12%', body:'🌙', fill:'95%'},
};
let _currentPreset = 'dawn';
let _dnStarTimer   = null;

function initDayNightPanel(){
  setTimePreset(_currentPreset || 'dawn', false);
  drawDnStars();
}

function setTimePreset(preset, applyMap=true){
  _currentPreset = preset;
  const p = TIME_PRESETS[preset];
  // 更新预设按钮
  document.querySelectorAll('.dn-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  const btn = document.getElementById('dnb-'+preset);
  if(btn) btn.classList.add('active');
  // 更新天空
  const sky = document.getElementById('dn-sky');
  if(sky) sky.style.background = `linear-gradient(180deg,${p.skyA},${p.skyB})`;
  // 更新天体
  const body = document.getElementById('dn-body');
  if(body){ body.textContent=p.body; body.style.left=`${parseFloat(p.fill)+2}%`; body.style.top=p.bodyY; }
  // 时间轴
  const fill = document.getElementById('dn-tl-fill');
  const dot  = document.getElementById('dn-tl-dot');
  if(fill) fill.style.width  = p.fill;
  if(dot)  dot.style.left   = p.fill;
  // 标题
  const title = document.getElementById('dn-panel-title');
  if(title) title.textContent = p.label+' 模式';
  // 当前时间显示
  const nowEl = document.getElementById('dn-now-time');
  if(nowEl) nowEl.textContent = `当前 ${String(p.hour).padStart(2,'0')}:00`;
  // 星星
  drawDnStars(preset==='night' || preset==='dawn');

  // 应用到地图
  if(applyMap){
    const isNightMode = (preset==='night');
    STATE.isNight = isNightMode;
    document.body.classList.toggle('night-mode', isNightMode);
    // 更新地图亮度
    const mapBg = document.getElementById('map-bg');
    const filters = {
      dawn:  'brightness(0.72) saturate(0.85) sepia(0.15) hue-rotate(-5deg)',
      day:   'brightness(1) saturate(1)',
      dusk:  'brightness(0.75) saturate(1.1) sepia(0.2) hue-rotate(5deg)',
      night: 'brightness(0.28) saturate(0.45) sepia(0.32) hue-rotate(195deg)',
    };
    if(mapBg) gsap.to(mapBg,{filter:filters[preset],duration:1.5,ease:'power2.inOut'});
    // 更新控制台图标
    const ico = document.getElementById('night-icon');
    const lbl = document.getElementById('night-lbl');
    const icons = {dawn:'🌅',day:'☀️',dusk:'🌇',night:'🌙'};
    if(ico){ ico.textContent=''; ico.className=''; ico.style.fontSize='18px'; ico.textContent=icons[preset]; }
    if(lbl) lbl.textContent = p.label.slice(2);
    // 星星效果
    document.querySelectorAll('.star').forEach(s=>{
      s.style.opacity = isNightMode ? (Math.random()*0.5+0.2).toFixed(2) : '0';
    });
    showToast(icons[preset],'视角切换', p.label+' 模式已应用');
  }
}

function drawDnStars(show=false){
  const cvs = document.getElementById('dn-star-cvs');
  if(!cvs) return;
  const ctx = cvs.getContext('2d');
  ctx.clearRect(0,0,cvs.width,cvs.height);
  if(!show) return;
  for(let i=0;i<40;i++){
    const x=(Math.sin(i*73.1)*.5+.5)*cvs.width;
    const y=(Math.cos(i*47.3)*.5+.5)*cvs.height*.7;
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x,y,.8+Math.random()*.8,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(220,235,255,${.3+Math.random()*.5})`; ctx.fill();
  }
}

// ── 组队面板 ──────────────────────────────────────
const TEAM_MEMBERS_DATA = [
  {name:'我（队长）',role:null,       avatar:'🧭',status:'online', score:null},
  {name:'探察员 小明', role:'eco',    avatar:'🌿',status:'online', score:340},
  {name:'参谋 阿红',   role:'red',    avatar:'🔥',status:'offline',score:210},
];
const ROLE_COLORS = {eco:'#3cdc60',red:'#e85030',blue:'#3888f0',null:'var(--gold)'};

function initTeamPanel(){
  // 生成随机队伍码
  const code = 'NS-' + Math.floor(1000+Math.random()*8999);
  const el = document.getElementById('team-code-display');
  if(el && el.textContent==='NS-2024') el.textContent = code;

  // 成员列表
  TEAM_MEMBERS_DATA[0].score = STATE.score;
  TEAM_MEMBERS_DATA[0].role  = STATE.role;
  const container = document.getElementById('team-members');
  if(!container) return;
  container.innerHTML = TEAM_MEMBERS_DATA.map((m,i)=>{
    const roleLabel = m.role ? {eco:'探察原境',red:'赓续红魂',blue:'彰扬侗韵'}[m.role] : '暂未选择';
    const col = ROLE_COLORS[m.role];
    return `<div class="tm-row">
      <div class="tm-avatar" style="background:${col}22;border-color:${col}44;">${m.avatar}</div>
      <div>
        <div class="tm-name">${m.name}${i===0?' <span style="font-size:9px;color:var(--gold);">👑</span>':''}</div>
        <div class="tm-role" style="color:${col};">${roleLabel}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="tm-status ${m.status}">${m.status==='online'?'在线':'离线'}</div>
      <div class="tm-score">${m.score!==null?m.score+' NSP':''}</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');

  // 进度条（完成POI数/总POI数）
  const pct = Math.round((STATE.completedPOIs.length / 6) * 100);
  const fill = document.getElementById('team-prog-fill');
  const pctEl= document.getElementById('team-prog-pct');
  if(fill) setTimeout(()=>fill.style.width=pct+'%',100);
  if(pctEl) pctEl.textContent = pct+'%';
}

function copyTeamCode(){
  const el = document.getElementById('team-code-display');
  if(!el) return;
  const code = el.textContent;
  // 复制到剪贴板
  if(navigator.clipboard){
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(code).then(()=>{
      showToast('📋','已复制','队伍码 '+code+' 已复制');
    });
  } else {
    showToast('📋','队伍码',code);
  }
}

function inviteTeam(){
  const link = `https://nanshan-tongdao.edu.cn/join?code=${document.getElementById('team-code-display').textContent}`;
  if(navigator.share){
    navigator.share({title:'南山·通道研学侦察队',text:'加入我的研学队伍！',url:link});
  } else {
    if(navigator.clipboard) navigator.clipboard.writeText(link);
    showToast('📨','邀请链接已复制','可分享给队友加入');
  }
}

function leaveTeam(){
  showToast('🚪','已退出队伍','您已离开当前侦察队');
  closePanel('team');
}

// ── GPS定位面板 ──────────────────────────────────────
// 南山·通道真实POI坐标参考
const GPS_POIS = [
  {name:'南山草原观景台', lat:26.1582, lon:109.7364, alt:1268},
  {name:'茅坪湖湿地入口', lat:26.2018, lon:109.8025, alt:892},
  {name:'老山界纪念碑',   lat:26.0845, lon:109.6892, alt:1542},
  {name:'紫阳峰顶',       lat:26.1256, lon:109.7628, alt:1836},
  {name:'皇都侗寨鼓楼',   lat:26.0432, lon:109.7255, alt:365},
  {name:'恭城书院',       lat:26.1938, lon:109.9012, alt:412},
];
const GPS_DIRS = ['正北','北偏东','正东','东偏南','正南','南偏西','正西','西偏北'];
let _gpsTimer  = null;
let _gpsFaked  = false; // 真实GPS是否可用

function initGPSPanel(){
  _gpsFaked = false;
  // 尝试真实GPS
  if(navigator.geolocation){
    navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(
      pos=>updateGPSDisplay(pos.coords.latitude, pos.coords.longitude, pos.coords.altitude||null, true),
      ()=>fakeGPS(),
      {timeout:4000, enableHighAccuracy:true}
    );
  } else {
    fakeGPS();
  }
  // 模拟方向变化
  _gpsTimer = setInterval(()=>{
    if(_openPanel==='gps' && _gpsFaked) fakeGPS(true);
  }, 5000);
}

function fakeGPS(silently=false){
  _gpsFaked = true;
  // 从POI列表随机选最近点
  const poi = GPS_POIS[Math.floor(Math.random()*GPS_POIS.length)];
  const latOff = (Math.random()-.5)*.002;
  const lonOff = (Math.random()-.5)*.002;
  updateGPSDisplay(poi.lat+latOff, poi.lon+lonOff, poi.alt+Math.round((Math.random()-.5)*20), false, poi);
}

function updateGPSDisplay(lat, lon, alt, isReal, nearPOI=null){
  const latEl  = document.getElementById('gps-lat');
  const lonEl  = document.getElementById('gps-lon');
  const altEl  = document.getElementById('gps-alt');
  const dirEl  = document.getElementById('gps-dir');
  const plEl   = document.getElementById('gps-place');
  const distEl = document.getElementById('gps-dist');
  const sigEl  = document.getElementById('gps-sig-txt');

  if(latEl) latEl.textContent = Math.abs(lat).toFixed(4)+'°'+(lat>=0?'N':'S');
  if(lonEl) lonEl.textContent = Math.abs(lon).toFixed(4)+'°'+(lon>=0?'E':'W');
  if(altEl && alt) altEl.textContent = Math.round(alt)+'m';

  const dirIdx = Math.floor(Math.random()*8);
  const deg    = Math.floor(Math.random()*360);
  if(dirEl) dirEl.textContent = GPS_DIRS[dirIdx]+' '+deg+'°';

  if(nearPOI){
    if(plEl)   plEl.textContent  = nearPOI.name;
    const dist = Math.floor(50+Math.random()*800);
    if(distEl) distEl.textContent = '约 '+dist+'m';
  }
  if(sigEl) sigEl.textContent = isReal ? '真实GPS' : '模拟';
}

function refreshGPS(){
  // 动画刷新
  const dot = document.querySelector('.gps-dot');
  if(dot){ dot.style.background='#f0d080'; setTimeout(()=>dot.style.background='#4cde88',800); }
  initGPSPanel();
  showToast('🔄','GPS刷新','正在重新获取坐标…');
}

function shareLocation(){
  const lat = document.getElementById('gps-lat')?.textContent || '';
  const lon = document.getElementById('gps-lon')?.textContent || '';
  const text = `我在南山·通道研学展馆 📍 ${lat}, ${lon}`;
  if(navigator.share){
    navigator.share({title:'我的研学位置',text});
  } else {
    if(navigator.clipboard) navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
    showToast('📤','位置已复制',lat+' '+lon);
  }
}

function toggleNight(){
  togglePanel('daynight');
}

let _openRPanel = null;

function toggleRPanel(name){
  if(_openRPanel === name){ closeRPanel(name); return; }
  if(_openRPanel) closeRPanel(_openRPanel, false);
  _openRPanel = name;
  const el = document.getElementById('rpanel-'+name);
  if(!el) return;
  el.classList.add('open');
  // 高亮导航按钮
  document.querySelectorAll('.rnav-btn').forEach(b=>b.style.borderColor='');
  const btn = document.getElementById('rnav-'+name);
  if(btn) btn.style.borderColor='rgba(201,168,76,0.55)';
  // 初始化内容
  if(name==='legend')  initLegendPanel();
  if(name==='task')    initTaskPanel();
  if(name==='bag')     initBagPanel();
  if(name==='profile') initProfilePanel();
  // 点外部关闭
  setTimeout(()=>{
    const handler = e=>{
      if(!el.contains(e.target) && !e.target.closest('.rnav-btn')){
        closeRPanel(name); document.removeEventListener('click', handler);
      }
    };
    document.addEventListener('click', handler);
  }, 150);
}

function closeRPanel(name, resetOpen=true){

  if(el) el.classList.remove('open');
  const btn = document.getElementById('rnav-'+name);
  if(btn) btn.style.borderColor='';
  if(resetOpen) _openRPanel = null;
}

// ── 图例面板 ────────────────────────────────────
function initLegendPanel(){
  const el = document.getElementById('leg-visited');
  if(el) el.textContent = STATE.completedPOIs.length;
}

// ── 任务面板 ────────────────────────────────────
// 将 POIS 中的所有任务展开为平铺列表，带完成状态
let _completedTasks = new Set(); // 已完成任务 key = poiKey+taskName
let _taskTab = 'all';

function initTaskPanel(){
  updateTaskRing();
  renderTaskList(_taskTab);
}

function switchTaskTab(tab){
  _taskTab = tab;
  ['all','doing','done'].forEach(t=>{
    const el = document.getElementById('ttab-'+t);
    if(el) el.classList.toggle('active', t===tab);
  });
  renderTaskList(tab);
}

function roleTasksFor(key){
  const role=STATE.role||'eco';
  const rt=(typeof POI_ROLE_TASKS!=='undefined')?POI_ROLE_TASKS[key]:null;
  let arr=[];
  if(rt){
    if(rt[role]&&rt[role].length) arr=arr.concat(rt[role].map(t=>({...t,grp:'role'})));
    if(rt.shared&&rt.shared.length) arr=arr.concat(rt.shared.map(t=>({...t,grp:'shared'})));
  }
  if(arr.length===0 && POIS[key]) arr=POIS[key].tasks.map(t=>({...t,grp:'role'}));
  return arr;
}
const POI_TYPE={nanshan:'eco',maoping:'eco',ziyang:'eco',laoshanjie:'red',gongcheng:'red',huangdu:'blue'};

function updateTaskRing(){
  let total=0; const doneSet=new Set();
  Object.keys(POIS).forEach(key=>{
    roleTasksFor(key).forEach(t=>{ const k=key+'_'+t.n; total++; if(_completedTasks.has(k)) doneSet.add(k); });
  });
  const done=doneSet.size;
  const pct=total>0?Math.round(done/total*100):0;
  const circle=document.getElementById('task-ring-circle');
  const pctEl=document.getElementById('task-ring-pct');
  const sumTxt=document.getElementById('task-summary-txt');
  const sumSub=document.getElementById('task-summary-sub');
  if(circle){ const circ=2*Math.PI*18; circle.style.strokeDashoffset=circ-circ*(pct/100); }
  if(pctEl) pctEl.textContent=pct+'%';
  if(sumTxt) sumTxt.textContent=done>0?`已完成 ${done}/${total} 个任务`:'尚未开始任务';
  if(sumSub) sumSub.textContent=done>0?`累计获得 ${STATE.score} NSP 积分`:('当前身份：'+(ROLE_LABELS[STATE.role||'eco'])+' · 完成任务可获 NSP');
}

function renderTaskList(tab){
  const container=document.getElementById('task-list-container');
  if(!container) return;
  const role=STATE.role||'eco';
  const TYPE_COLOR={eco:'rgba(40,180,70,0.25)',red:'rgba(200,50,30,0.25)',blue:'rgba(40,120,240,0.25)'};
  const TYPE_ICON ={eco:'🌿',red:'🔥',blue:'💙'};
  let html='';
  Object.entries(POIS).forEach(([key, poi])=>{
    const type=POI_TYPE[key]||'eco';
    const arr=roleTasksFor(key).map(t=>({...t, key:key+'_'+t.n, poi:poi.t, type}));
    const filtered=arr.filter(t=>{ const done=_completedTasks.has(t.key); if(tab==='done')return done; if(tab==='doing')return !done; return true; });
    if(filtered.length===0) return;
    html+=`<div class="task-group-title">${TYPE_ICON[type]} ${poi.t}</div>`;
    filtered.forEach(t=>{
      const done=_completedTasks.has(t.key);
      const tag = t.grp==='shared' ? '<span class="tr-tag shared">全员</span>' : `<span class="tr-tag role">${ROLE_LABELS[role]}</span>`;
      html+=`<div class="task-row ${done?'done':''}" onclick="doTaskFromPanel('${key}','${t.n}',${t.p},'${t.key}')">
        <div class="tr-icon-wrap" style="background:${TYPE_COLOR[type]};">${t.i}</div>
        <div class="tr-info"><strong>${t.n} ${tag}</strong><span>${t.d}</span></div>
        <div class="tr-pts">${done?'':'+'} ${t.p}</div>
        <div class="tr-check">${done?'✅':'⬜'}</div>
      </div>`;
    });
  });
  if(html==='') html='<div class="bag-empty">暂无'+{all:'',doing:'进行中',done:'已完成'}[tab]+'任务</div>';
  container.innerHTML = html;
}

function doTaskFromPanel(poiKey, taskName, pts, taskKey){
  if(_completedTasks.has(taskKey)){
    showToast('ℹ️','任务已完成',taskName+' 已完成过');
    return;
  }
  _completedTasks.add(taskKey);
  addScore(pts);
  showToast('✅','任务完成', taskName+' +'+pts+'NSP');
  updateTaskRing();
  renderTaskList(_taskTab);
  if(Math.random()>0.45) setTimeout(triggerSp, 800);
}

// ── 背包面板 ────────────────────────────────────
// 收集到的物种/道具/勋章
let BAG = {
  species: [],  // SPECIES 对象列表
  items: [
    {ico:'🔭',name:'望远镜',desc:'观察远处生物，识别距离提升50%。',rarity:'普通',rarityColor:'#888'},
    {ico:'📓',name:'研学手册',desc:'记录研学笔记，任务提示更清晰。',rarity:'普通',rarityColor:'#888'},

  ],

};
const MEDALS_DEF = [
  {ico:'🏅',name:'初探者',desc:'完成首个POI探索',unlocked:false,rarityColor:'#888'},
  {ico:'🌿',name:'生态卫士',desc:'完成所有生态任务',unlocked:false,rarityColor:'#3cdc60'},
  {ico:'⭐',name:'红色传承',desc:'完成所有红色任务',unlocked:false,rarityColor:'#e85030'},

let _bagTab = 'species';

function initBagPanel(){
  // 根据完成情况更新勋章
  MEDALS_DEF[0].unlocked = STATE.completedPOIs.length>0;
  MEDALS_DEF[4].unlocked = _completedTasks.size >= 18;
  switchBagTab(_bagTab);
}

function switchBagTab(tab){
  _bagTab = tab;
  ['species','items','medals'].forEach(t=>{
    const el=document.getElementById('btab-'+t);
    if(el) el.classList.toggle('active',t===tab);
  });
  renderBagContent(tab);
}

function renderBagContent(tab){
  const el = document.getElementById('bag-content');
  if(!el) return;
  if(tab==='species'){
    if(BAG.species.length===0){
      el.innerHTML='<div class="bag-empty">🔍<br>尚未发现物种<br><span style="font-size:10px;opacity:0.6;">探索POI可随机触发物种图鉴</span></div>';
      return;
    }
    el.innerHTML='<div class="bag-grid">'+
      BAG.species.map(s=>`<div class="bag-item" onclick="showBagDetail('${s.ic}','${s.n}','${s.d}','${s.gr}','${s.gc}')">
        <div class="bi-icon">${s.ic}</div>
        <div class="bi-name">${s.n}</div>
      </div>`).join('')+
    '</div>';
  } else if(tab==='items'){
    el.innerHTML='<div class="bag-grid">'+
      BAG.items.map(it=>`<div class="bag-item" onclick="showBagDetail('${it.ico}','${it.name}','${it.desc}','${it.rarity}','${it.rarityColor}')">
        <div class="bi-icon">${it.ico}</div>
        <div class="bi-name">${it.name}</div>
      </div>`).join('')+
    '</div>';
  } else {
    el.innerHTML='<div class="bag-grid">'+
      MEDALS_DEF.map(m=>`<div class="bag-item ${m.unlocked?'':'locked'}" onclick="${m.unlocked?`showBagDetail('${m.ico}','${m.name}','${m.desc}','勋章','${m.rarityColor}')`:''}"
        title="${m.unlocked?m.name:'???'}">
        <div class="bi-icon">${m.ico}</div>
        <div class="bi-name">${m.unlocked?m.name:'???'}</div>
      </div>`).join('')+
    '</div>';
  }
}

function showBagDetail(icon, name, desc, rarity, color){
  document.getElementById('bd-icon').textContent = icon;
  document.getElementById('bd-name').textContent = name;
  document.getElementById('bd-desc').textContent = desc;
  const rEl = document.getElementById('bd-rarity');
  rEl.textContent = rarity;
  rEl.style.cssText = `color:${color};background:${color}22;border:1px solid ${color}55;`;
  document.getElementById('bag-detail-ov').classList.add('show');
}
function closeBagDetail(){
  document.getElementById('bag-detail-ov').classList.remove('show');
}

// 物种触发时同步加入背包
const _origTriggerSp = triggerSp;
function triggerSp(){
  const sp = SPECIES[Math.floor(Math.random()*SPECIES.length)];
  // 加入背包（去重）
  if(!BAG.species.find(s=>s.n===sp.n)) BAG.species.push(sp);
  // 原有物种弹窗逻辑
  document.getElementById('sp-head').style.background=`linear-gradient(135deg,${sp.gc}22,${sp.gc}44)`;
  document.getElementById('sp-gr').textContent=sp.gr;
  document.getElementById('sp-gr').style.color=sp.gc;
  document.getElementById('sp-gr').style.borderColor=sp.gc;
  document.getElementById('sp-ico').textContent=sp.ic;
  document.getElementById('sp-nm').textContent=sp.n;
  document.getElementById('sp-sc').textContent=sp.sc;
  document.getElementById('sp-ds').textContent=sp.d;
  document.getElementById('sp-pt').innerHTML=`🌿 新增 <strong>+${sp.p}</strong> NSP · 已录入生态图鉴`;
  document.getElementById('sp-ov').classList.add('show');
  addScore(sp.p);
}

const ROLE_META = {
  eco:{label:'探察原境',color:'#3cdc60',avatar:'🌿'},
  red:{label:'赓续红魂',color:'#e85030',avatar:'🔥'},
  blue:{label:'彰扬侗韵',color:'#3888f0',avatar:'💙'},
};
const LEVEL_THRESHOLDS = [0,100,300,600,1000,1800,3000];
const LEVEL_NAMES = ['初级探察员','见习侦察员','资深侦察员','精英侦察员','王牌侦察员','传奇侦察员','南山传承者'];

function initProfilePanel(){
  const score = STATE.score;
  const role  = STATE.role;
  // 头像&身份
  const avatar = document.getElementById('prof-avatar');
  const roleTag= document.getElementById('prof-role-tag');
  const levEl  = document.getElementById('prof-level');
  if(role && ROLE_META[role]){
    const m = ROLE_META[role];
    if(avatar)  { avatar.textContent=m.avatar; avatar.style.borderColor=m.color+'66'; }
    if(roleTag) { roleTag.textContent=m.label; roleTag.style.cssText=`color:${m.color};background:${m.color}22;border:1px solid ${m.color}44;border-radius:10px;padding:2px 10px;font-size:10px;`; }
  }
  // 等级
  let lv=0;
  for(let i=0;i<LEVEL_THRESHOLDS.length;i++) if(score>=LEVEL_THRESHOLDS[i]) lv=i;
  if(levEl) levEl.textContent = `Lv.${lv+1} · ${LEVEL_NAMES[lv]}`;
  // 积分环
  const arc = document.getElementById('score-ring-arc');
  const numEl= document.getElementById('prof-score');
  if(numEl) numEl.textContent = score;
  if(arc){
    const maxScore = 2000;
    const pct = Math.min(score/maxScore, 1);
    const circ = 2*Math.PI*28;
    arc.style.strokeDashoffset = circ - circ*pct;
  }
  // 分类积分（简单分配）
  const ecoScore  = Math.floor(score*(role==='eco'?0.6:0.2));
  const redScore  = Math.floor(score*(role==='red'?0.6:0.2));
  const blueScore = score - ecoScore - redScore;
  const maxSub = Math.max(ecoScore, redScore, blueScore, 1);
  [{id:'eco',val:ecoScore},{id:'red',val:redScore},{id:'blue',val:blueScore}].forEach(({id,val})=>{
    const vEl = document.getElementById(`prof-${id}-score`);
    const bEl = document.getElementById(`prof-${id}-bar`);
    if(vEl) vEl.textContent = val;
    if(bEl) setTimeout(()=>bEl.style.width=(val/maxSub*100)+'%', 100);
  });
  // 成就
  MEDALS_DEF[0].unlocked = STATE.completedPOIs.length>0;
  MEDALS_DEF[4].unlocked = _completedTasks.size>=18;
  const achGrid = document.getElementById('ach-grid');
  if(achGrid) achGrid.innerHTML = MEDALS_DEF.map(m=>`
    <div class="ach-item ${m.unlocked?'unlocked':'locked'}" title="${m.unlocked?m.name+'：'+m.desc:'???'}">
      <div class="ai-ico">${m.ico}</div>
      <div class="ai-lbl">${m.unlocked?m.name:'???'}</div>
    </div>`).join('');
  // 研学记录
  const records = [
    {ico:'📍',name:'探索点位',sub:'已访问POI',val:STATE.completedPOIs.length+'/6'},
    {ico:'✅',name:'完成任务',sub:'所有分类',val:_completedTasks.size+'/18'},
    {ico:'🦎',name:'物种发现',sub:'生态图鉴',val:BAG.species.length+'/'+SPECIES.length},
    {ico:'⏱️',name:'研学时长',sub:'本次会话',val:Math.floor((Date.now()-_sessionStart)/60000)+'分钟'},
  ];
  const srEl = document.getElementById('study-records');
  if(srEl) srEl.innerHTML = records.map(r=>`
    <div class="sr-item">
      <div class="sr-icon">${r.ico}</div>
      <div class="sr-info"><strong>${r.name}</strong><span>${r.sub}</span></div>
      <div class="sr-val">${r.val}</div>
    </div>`).join('');
}
const _sessionStart = Date.now();

// ── 进入彰扬侗韵世界 ──────────────────────────────
let _blueAudio = null;
let _blueInited = false;

function enterBlueWorld(){
  showAct('act-blue');

  const tl = gsap.timeline();

  // 0~2s 镜头飞向皇都侗寨（背景Canvas动画）
  initBlueBgCanvas();

  // 1.5s 晨雾浮现
  tl.fromTo('.blue-fog', {opacity:0}, {opacity:1, duration:1.5, ease:'power2.out'}, 0.5);

  // 2~3s 顶部导航栏下滑
  tl.fromTo('#blue-topbar', {opacity:0, y:-20}, {opacity:1, y:0, duration:0.8, ease:'power2.out'}, 1.5);

  // 2.5~4s 鼓楼框架从雾中浮现
  tl.fromTo('#drum-tower-frame',
    {opacity:0, scale:0.88, filter:'blur(12px)'},
    {opacity:1, scale:1, filter:'blur(0px)', duration:1.8, ease:'power2.out'},
    2.0
  );

  // 3.5s Tab出现
  tl.fromTo('#blue-tabs', {opacity:0, y:20}, {opacity:1, y:0, duration:0.7, ease:'back.out(1.2)'}, 3.2);

  // 4s 侗族大歌响起
  tl.call(()=>{
    playDongSong();
    if(!_blueInited){ _blueInited=true; initBrocadeSection(); initFeastSection(); initWorkshopSection(); }
  }, null, 3.8);
}

// ── 全屏背景Canvas（鸟瞰飞行→鼓楼视角） ──────────
function initBlueBgCanvas(){
  const cvs = document.getElementById('blue-bg-canvas');
  if(!cvs||cvs._running) return;
  cvs._running = true;
  cvs.width = window.innerWidth; cvs.height = window.innerHeight;
  window.addEventListener('resize',()=>{cvs.width=window.innerWidth;cvs.height=window.innerHeight;});
  const ctx = cvs.getContext('2d'); let t=0;

  function frame(){
    t += 0.25; const w=cvs.width, h=cvs.height;
    ctx.clearRect(0,0,w,h);
    // 夜空渐变
    const sky=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,h);
    sky.addColorStop(0,'#010208'); sky.addColorStop(0.45,'#040c20'); sky.addColorStop(1,'#060e2a');
    ctx.fillStyle=sky; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
    // 月光
    const mx=w*.72, my=h*.12;
    const mg=ctx.createRadialGradient(mx,my,0,mx,my,h*.5);
    mg.addColorStop(0,'rgba(160,200,255,0.28)'); mg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
    ctx.fillStyle=mg; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(mx,my,16,0,Math.PI*2);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(210,235,255,0.85)'; ctx.fill();
    // 星点
    for(let i=0;i<45;i++){
      const sx=(Math.sin(i*73.1)*.5+.5)*w, sy=(Math.cos(i*47.3)*.5+.5)*h*.55;
      const fl=.25+Math.sin(t*.05+i*1.3)*.2;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(sx,sy,.9,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.fillStyle=`rgba(200,225,255,${fl})`; ctx.fill();
    }
    // 远山（侗寨背景）
    [
      [.58,h*.22,.85,'rgba(8,18,42,0.92)',.009],
      [.68,h*.17,.6, 'rgba(10,22,48,0.96)',.013],
      [.78,h*.12,.4, 'rgba(5,12,32,1.00)', .006],
    ].forEach(([yb,amp,freq,col,spd])=>{
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0,h);
      for(let x=0;x<=w;x+=2){
        const n=Math.sin(x*freq*.003+spd*t)*.5+Math.sin(x*freq*.007+spd*t*.7)*.3;
        ctx.lineTo(x, h*yb-(n*.5+.5)*amp);
      }
      ctx.lineTo(w,h); ctx.closePath(); ctx.fillStyle=col; ctx.fill();
    });
    // 灯火（村寨点点灯光）
    for(let i=0;i<22;i++){
      const lx=(Math.sin(i*82.3)*.5+.5)*w*.8+w*.1;
      const ly=h*(.62+Math.sin(i*.8)*.05);
      const lf=.4+Math.sin(t*.06+i*1.2)*.25;
      const lg=ctx.createRadialGradient(lx,ly,0,lx,ly,16+i%4*4);
      lg.addColorStop(0,`rgba(255,200,80,${lf})`); lg.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.fillStyle=lg; ctx.fillRect(lx-20,ly-20,40,40);
    }
    // 云雾（低层飘浮）
    ctx.save(); ctx.globalAlpha=0.45;
    for(let i=0;i<10;i++){
      const cx=((i*138.5+t*.15)%w);
      const cy=h*(.55+Math.sin(i*.7)*.06);
      const rx=100+i*22, ry=20+i*4;
      const g=ctx.createRadialGradient(cx,cy,0,cx,cy,rx);
      g.addColorStop(0,'rgba(180,210,255,0.18)'); g.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.save(); ctx.scale(1,ry/rx);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(cx,cy*(rx/ry),rx,0,Math.PI*2); ctx.fillStyle=g; ctx.fill();
      ctx.restore();
    }
    ctx.restore();
    requestAnimationFrame(frame);
  }
  frame();
}

// ── 侗族大歌（Web Audio API合成） ──────────────────
function playDongSong(){
  try{
    const AC = window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext;
    if(!AC) return;
    _blueAudio = new AC();
    const ctx = _blueAudio;
    // 多声部：低音持续音 + 中音旋律 + 高音泛音
    function tone(freq, start, dur, vol=0.12, type='sine'){
      const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
      const gain= ctx.createGain();
      osc.connect(gain); gain.connect(ctx.destination);
      osc.type=type; osc.frequency.value=freq;
      gain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, ctx.currentTime+start);
      gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(vol, ctx.currentTime+start+0.5);
      gain.gain.setValueAtTime(vol, ctx.currentTime+start+dur-0.5);
      gain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, ctx.currentTime+start+dur);
      osc.start(ctx.currentTime+start);
      osc.stop(ctx.currentTime+start+dur);
    }
    // 侗族五声音阶风格（宫商角徵羽）：Do Re Mi Sol La
    const scale=[261.6,293.7,329.6,392,440,523.3,587.3,659.3];
    // 低音持续
    [0,4,8,12].forEach(s=>{ tone(130.8,s,4.5,0.08,'sine'); tone(164.8,s,4.5,0.06,'sine'); });
    // 中音旋律（简单循环）
    [[0,0],[2,0.8],[1,1.6],[4,2.4],[3,3.2],[0,4.0],
     [2,5.0],[4,5.8],[3,6.6],[1,7.4],[2,8.2],[0,9.0]].forEach(([i,s])=>{
      tone(scale[i], s, 0.9, 0.1, 'sine');
    });
    // 高音泛音
    [[5,0.4],[6,2.8],[7,5.2],[5,7.6]].forEach(([i,s])=>{
      tone(scale[i], s, 1.8, 0.05, 'sine');
    });
    // 显示音乐指示
    const ind=document.getElementById('music-indicator');
    if(ind){ ind.classList.add('show'); setTimeout(()=>ind.classList.remove('show'),12000); }
    addScore(50);
    showToast('🎵','侗族大歌','天籁之音缓缓响起 +50 NSP');
  } catch(e){ console.log('Audio not available'); }
}

// ── Tab切换 ──────────────────────────────────────
function switchBlueTab(tab){
  ['brocade','feast','workshop'].forEach(t=>{
    const sec=document.getElementById('bs-'+t);
    const btn=document.getElementById('btt-'+t);
    if(sec){ sec.classList.toggle('active', t===tab); }
    if(btn){ btn.classList.toggle('active', t===tab); }
  });
}

// ════════════════════════════════════
//  侗锦密码
// ════════════════════════════════════
function initBrocadeSection(){
  const grid = document.getElementById('pattern-grid');
  if(!grid||grid.children.length>0) return;
  grid.innerHTML = BROCADE_PATTERNS.map(p=>`
    <div class="pattern-card" id="pc-${p.id}" onclick="selectPattern('${p.id}')">
      <canvas id="pcvs-${p.id}" width="80" height="80"></canvas>
      <div class="pc-name">${p.name}</div>
    </div>
  `).join('');
  // 绘制各纹样缩略图
  BROCADE_PATTERNS.forEach(p=>{
    const cvs=document.getElementById('pcvs-'+p.id);
    if(cvs) drawPatternThumb(cvs, p);
  });
}

function drawPatternThumb(cvs, p){
  const ctx=cvs.getContext('2d'), w=cvs.width, h=cvs.height;
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(6,14,40,1)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
  const cols=p.colors; const rows=8, colsN=8;
  const cw=w/colsN, ch=h/rows;
  // 按纹样ID绘制特征图案
  const patterns={
    dragon:(r,c)=> (r+c)%3===0||Math.abs(r-c)===2,
    mountain:(r,c)=> r<=c&&r<=(rows-1-c)||r===c,
    bird:(r,c)=> r===4-Math.abs(c-4)||c===4,
    flower:(r,c)=> (r%2===0&&c%2===0)||((r+c)%4===0),
    water:(r,c)=> Math.sin((r+c)*0.8)>0.3,
    totem:(r,c)=> r===c||r===(rows-1-c)||r===rows/2||c===colsN/2,
  };
  const fn=patterns[p.id]||(()=>false);
  for(let r=0;r<rows;r++) for(let c=0;c<colsN;c++){
    ctx.fillStyle = fn(r,c) ? cols[Math.floor(Math.random()*3)] : cols[3+Math.floor(Math.random()*3)];
    ctx.fillRect(c*cw+0.5, r*ch+0.5, cw-1, ch-1);
  }
}

function drawPatternDetail(cvs, p){
  const ctx=cvs.getContext('2d'), w=cvs.width, h=cvs.height;
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(4,10,30,1)'; ctx.fillRect(0,0,w,h);
  const cols=p.colors; const rows=10, colsN=18;
  const cw=w/colsN, ch=h/rows;
  const patterns={
    dragon:(r,c)=> (r+c*2)%5===0||(Math.abs(r-4)===1&&c%3!==0),
    mountain:(r,c)=> r===9-Math.floor(c/2)||r===9-Math.floor((colsN-1-c)/2),
    bird:(r,c)=> Math.abs(r-4)===Math.abs(c-9)||r===4&&Math.abs(c-9)<4,
    flower:(r,c)=> (r%3===1&&c%3===1)||(r%3===0&&c%3===2),
    water:(r,c)=> Math.floor(Math.sin((r*2+c)*0.6)*1.5+1.5)===1,
    totem:(r,c)=> r===c%rows||r===(rows-1-c%rows)||r===rows/2,
  };
  const fn=patterns[p.id]||(()=>false);
  for(let r=0;r<rows;r++) for(let c=0;c<colsN;c++){
    ctx.fillStyle = fn(r,c) ? cols[r%cols.length] : cols[(r+3)%cols.length];
    ctx.fillRect(c*cw+0.5, r*ch+0.5, cw-1, ch-1);
  }
}

let _decomposeTimer=null;
function selectPattern(id){
  const p=BROCADE_PATTERNS.find(x=>x.id===id);
  if(!p) return;
  // 选中高亮
  document.querySelectorAll('.pattern-card').forEach(c=>c.classList.remove('selected'));
  const card=document.getElementById('pc-'+id); if(card) card.classList.add('selected');
  // 隐藏占位，显示详情
  document.getElementById('bd-placeholder').style.display='none';
  const info=document.getElementById('brocade-info');
  info.classList.add('show');
  // 绘制大图
  const detCvs=document.getElementById('bi-detail-canvas');
  if(detCvs) drawPatternDetail(detCvs, p);
  // 拆解动画
  clearTimeout(_decomposeTimer);
  const track=document.getElementById('decompose-track');
  track.innerHTML=p.units.map((u,i)=>`
    <div class="dc-unit" id="dcu-${i}">${u}</div>
    ${i<p.units.length-1?'<div class="dc-arrow">→</div>':''}
  `).join('');
  p.units.forEach((_,i)=>{
    _decomposeTimer=setTimeout(()=>{
      const el=document.getElementById('dcu-'+i); if(el) el.classList.add('revealed');
    }, i*400);
  });
  // 信息卡片
  const cards=document.getElementById('bi-info-cards');
  cards.innerHTML=`
    <div class="bi-card">
      <div class="bi-card-label">纹样含义</div>
      <div class="bi-card-val">${p.meaning}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="bi-card">
      <div class="bi-card-label">图腾来源</div>
      <div class="bi-card-val">${p.origin}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="bi-card">
      <div class="bi-card-label">制作工艺</div>
      <div class="bi-card-val">${p.craft}</div>
    </div>
  `;
  addScore(10);
}

// ════════════════════════════════════
function initFeastSection(){
  const container=document.getElementById('feast-dishes');
  if(!container||container.children.length>0) return;
  // 注入菜品卡（绝对定位叠在桌面SVG上）
  const wrap=document.getElementById('feast-table-wrap');
  FEAST_DISHES.forEach((d,i)=>{
    const div=document.createElement('div');
    div.className='dish-card'; div.id='dish-'+i;
    div.style.left=d.pos.left; div.style.top=d.pos.top;
    div.onclick=()=>showDishStory(i);
    div.innerHTML=`<div class="dish-icon">${d.icon}</div><div class="dish-label">${d.name}</div>`;
    wrap.appendChild(div);
    // 延迟弹出动画
    setTimeout(()=>{
      gsap.fromTo(div,{opacity:0,scale:0,y:20},{opacity:1,scale:1,y:0,duration:0.55,ease:'back.out(1.7)'});
    }, i*180+400);
  });
}

function showDishStory(i){
  const d=FEAST_DISHES[i];
  document.getElementById('ds-icon').textContent=d.icon;
  document.getElementById('ds-name').textContent=d.name;
  document.getElementById('ds-sub').textContent=d.sub;
  document.getElementById('ds-text').textContent=d.story;
  document.getElementById('ds-tags').innerHTML=d.tags.map(t=>`<span class="ds-tag">${t}</span>`).join('');
  document.getElementById('dish-story').classList.add('show');
  addScore(15);
}
function closeDishStory(){ document.getElementById('dish-story').classList.remove('show'); }
